 or unke munh se gaaliyon kii bauchhaar, unke apane deshi takiyakalamon ke saath

 And then you are mentally prepared for bad abuses
 par pannon main gaaliyaan kab aati hai, or aap sanvaadon ke saath usko hajam kar jate hai, aapako pataa bhi nahin chalata

 upanyaas ‘chirkut das chingaari’ kii bhashaa bahut hi saral-sahaj or ganwai shabdaawaliyon se bhari hui he

 ‘saliana muskaan’, ‘yadi maan l ki jadi’, ‘navalanth’, ‘pahenta-chaheti’, ‘chirik den ki palapal den’, ‘chutarachahent’, ‘ramras’, ‘pardaafphaas’, ‘balistor’, ‘lathumma express’, ‘figureyman’, ‘iks’, ‘laundiastic’, ‘galati par singhia maangur ho janaa’, ‘kanfioverdence’, ye saare alfaaz aapako gaanvon kii saiyr par liye chalate hai

 Conflict lacks centrality in the narrative

 yphone ke steps baad main bataaenge
 Android users can also wipe data

 --- Navigate to Find My Device by going to Settings and from here give location access to your device
 --- settings main find maay divaais ko hameshaa aneble rakhen

 agar aapke paas doosraa mobile he usamen find maay divaais downlod karke bhi acces kar sakate hai
 --- Here you will see the list of devices connected to it
